<s> japan opened its ports after signing the treaty of kanagawa with the us in 1854 and began to intensively modernize and industrialize <\s>
<s> during the late 19th and early 20th centuries japan became a regional power that was able to defeat the forces of both china and russia <\s>
<s> it occupied korea formosa taiwan and southern sakhalin island <\s>
<s> in 1931-32 japan occupied manchuria and in 1937 it launched a full-scale invasion of china <\s>
<s> japan attacked us forces in 1941 triggering america's entry into world war ii and soon occupied much of east and southeast asia <\s>
<s> after its defeat in world war ii japan recovered to become an economic power and an ally of the us <\s>
<s> while the emperor retains his throne as a symbol of national unity elected politicians hold actual decision-making power <\s>
<s> following three decades of unprecedented growth japan's economy experienced a major slowdown starting in the 1990s but the country remains a major economic power <\s>
<s> jersey jersey and the other channel islands represent the last remnants of the medieval dukedom of normandy that held sway in both france and england <\s>
<s> these islands were the only british soil occupied by german troops in world war ii <\s>
<s> jersey is a british crown dependency but is not part of the uk or of the european union <\s>
<s> however the uk government is constitutionally responsible for its defense and international representation <\s>
<s> jordan following world war i and the dissolution of the ottoman empire the uk received a mandate to govern much of the middle east <\s>
<s> britain separated out a semi-autonomous region of transjordan from palestine in the early 1920s and the area gained its independence in 1946 it adopted the name of jordan in 1950 <\s>
<s> the country's long-time ruler was king hussein 1953-99 <\s>
<s> a pragmatic leader he successfully navigated competing pressures from the major powers us ussr and uk various arab states israel and a large internal palestinian population <\s>
<s> jordan lost the west bank to israel in the 1967 war and barely managed to defeat palestinian rebels who attempted to overthrow the monarchy in 1970 <\s>
<s> king hussein in 1988 permanently relinquished jordanian claims to the west bank <\s>
<s> in 1989 he reinstituted parliamentary elections and initiated a gradual political liberalization political parties were legalized in 1992 <\s>
<s> in 1994 he signed a peace treaty with israel <\s>
<s> king abdallah ii the son of king hussein assumed the throne following his father's death in february 1999 <\s>
<s> since then he has consolidated his power and undertaken an aggressive economic reform program <\s>
<s> jordan acceded to the world trade organization in 2000 and began to participate in the european free trade association in 2001 <\s>
<s> in 2003 jordan staunchly supported the coalition ouster of saddam in iraq and following the outbreak of insurgent violence in iraq absorbed thousands of displaced iraqis <\s>
<s> municipal elections were held in july 2007 under a system in which 20 of seats in all municipal councils were reserved by quota for women <\s>
<s> parliamentary elections were held in november 2010 and saw independent pro-government candidates win the vast majority of seats <\s>
<s> kazakhstan ethnic kazakhs a mix of turkic and mongol nomadic tribes who migrated into the region in the 13th century were rarely united as a single nation <\s>
<s> the area was conquered by russia in the 18th century and kazakhstan became a soviet republic in 1936 <\s>
<s> during the 1950s and 1960s agricultural virgin lands program soviet citizens were encouraged to help cultivate kazakhstan's northern pastures <\s>
<s> this influx of immigrants mostly russians but also some other deported nationalities skewed the ethnic mixture and enabled non-ethnic kazakhs to outnumber natives <\s>
<s> independence in 1991 drove many of these newcomers to emigrate <\s>
<s> kazakhstan's economy is larger than those of all the other central asian states largely due to the country's vast natural resources <\s>
<s> current issues include developing a cohesive national identity expanding the development of the country's vast energy resources and exporting them to world markets diversifying the economy outside the oil gas and mining sectors enhancing kazakhstan's economic competitiveness developing a multiparty parliament and advancing political and social reform and strengthening relations with neighboring states and other foreign powers <\s>
<s> kenya founding president and liberation struggle icon jomo kenyatta led kenya from independence in 1963 until his death in 1978 when president daniel toroitich arap moi took power in a constitutional succession <\s>
<s> the country was a de facto one-party state from 1969 until 1982 when the ruling kenya african national union kanu made itself the sole legal party in kenya <\s>
<s> moi acceded to internal and external pressure for political liberalization in late 1991 <\s>
<s> the ethnically fractured opposition failed to dislodge kanu from power in elections in 1992 and 1997 which were marred by violence and fraud but were viewed as having generally reflected the will of the kenyan people <\s>
<s> president moi stepped down in december 2002 following fair and peaceful elections <\s>
<s> mwai kibaki running as the candidate of the multiethnic united opposition group the national rainbow coalition narc defeated kanu candidate uhuru kenyatta and assumed the presidency following a campaign centered on an anticorruption platform <\s>
<s> kibaki's narc coalition splintered in 2005 over the constitutional review process <\s>
<s> government defectors joined with kanu to form a new opposition coalition the orange democratic movement which defeated the government's draft constitution in a popular referendum in november 2005 <\s>
<s> kibaki's reelection in december 2007 brought charges of vote rigging from odm candidate raila odinga and unleashed two months of violence in which as many as 1,500 people died <\s>
<s> un-sponsored talks in late february produced a powersharing accord bringing odinga into the government in the restored position of prime minister <\s>
<s> kiribati the gilbert islands became a british protectorate in 1892 and a colony in 1915 they were captured by the japanese in the pacific war in 1941 <\s>
<s> the islands of makin and tarawa were the sites of major us amphibious victories over entrenched japanese garrisons in 1943 <\s>
<s> the gilbert islands were granted self-rule by the uk in 1971 and complete independence in 1979 under the new name of kiribati <\s>
<s> the us relinquished all claims to the sparsely inhabited phoenix and line island groups in a 1979 treaty of friendship with kiribati <\s>
<s> korea north an independent kingdom for much of its long history korea was occupied by japan beginning in 1905 following the russo-japanese war <\s>
<s> five years later japan formally annexed the entire peninsula <\s>
<s> following world war ii korea was split with the northern half coming under soviet-sponsored communist control <\s>
<s> after failing in the korean war 1950-53 to conquer the us-backed republic of korea rok in the southern portion by force north korea dprk under its founder president kim il sung adopted a policy of ostensible diplomatic and economic self-reliance as a check against outside influence <\s>
<s> the dprk demonized the us as the ultimate threat to its social system through state-funded propaganda and molded political economic and military policies around the core ideological objective of eventual unification of korea under pyongyang's control <\s>
<s> kim's son the current ruler kim jong il was officially designated as his father's successor in 1980 assuming a growing political and managerial role until the elder kim's death in 1994 <\s>
<s> after decades of economic mismanagement and resource misallocation the dprk since the mid 1990s has relied heavily on international aid to feed its population <\s>
<s> north korea's history of regional military provocations proliferation of military-related items long-range missile development wmd programs including tests of nuclear devices in 2006 and 2009 and massive conventional armed forces are of major concern to the international community <\s>
<s> korea south an independent korean state or collection of states has existed almost continuously for several millennia <\s>
<s> between its initial unification in the 7th century from three predecessor korean states until the 20th century korea existed as a single independent country <\s>
<s> in 1905 following the russo-japanese war korea became a protectorate of imperial japan and in 1910 it was annexed as a colony <\s>
<s> korea regained its independence following japan's surrender to the united states in 1945 <\s>
<s> after world war ii a republic of korea rok was set up in the southern half of the korean peninsula while a communist-style government was installed in the north the dprk <\s>
<s> during the korean war 1950-53 us troops and un forces fought alongside soldiers from the rok to defend south korea from dprk attacks supported by china and the soviet union <\s>
<s> an armistice was signed in 1953 splitting the peninsula along a demilitarized zone at about the 38th parallel <\s>
<s> thereafter south korea achieved rapid economic growth with per capita income rising to roughly 17 times the level of north korea <\s>
<s> in 1993 kim young-sam became south korea's first civilian president following 32 years of military rule <\s>
<s> in keeping with the framework established at the madrid conference in october 1991 bilateral negotiations were conducted between israel and palestinian representatives and syria to achieve a permanent settlement <\s>
<s> israel and palestinian officials signed on 13 september 1993 a declaration of principles also known as the oslo accords guiding an interim period of palestinian self-rule <\s>
<s> outstanding territorial and other disputes with jordan were resolved in the 26 october 1994 israel-jordan treaty of peace <\s>
<s> in addition on 25 may 2000 israel withdrew unilaterally from southern lebanon which it had occupied since 1982 <\s>
<s> in april 2003 us president bush working in conjunction with the eu un and russia the quartet took the lead in laying out a roadmap to a final settlement of the conflict by 2005 based on reciprocal steps by the two parties leading to two states israel and a democratic palestine <\s>
<s> however progress toward a permanent status agreement was undermined by israeli-palestinian violence between september 2003 and february 2005 <\s>
<s> in the summer of 2005 israel unilaterally disengaged from the gaza strip evacuating settlers and its military while retaining control over most points of entry into the gaza strip <\s>
<s> the election of hamas to head the palestinian legislative council froze relations between israel and the palestinian authority pa <\s>
<s> ehud olmert became prime minister in march 2006 and presided over a 34 day conflict with hizballah in lebanon in june-august 2006 and a 23 day conflict with hamas in the gaza strip during december 2008 and january 2009 <\s>
<s> olmert who in june 2007 resumed talks with pa president mahmoud abbas resigned in september 2008 <\s>
<s> prime minister binyamin netanyahu formed a coalition in march 2009 following a february 2009 general election <\s>
<s> direct talks launched in september 2010 collapsed following the expiration of israel's 10 month partial settlement construction moratorium in the west bank <\s>
<s> diplomatic initiatives to revive the negotiations through proximity talks began at the end of 2010 <\s>
<s> italy italy became a nation-state in 1861 when the regional states of the peninsula along with sardinia and sicily were united under king victor emmanuel ii <\s>
<s> an era of parliamentary government came to a close in the early 1920s when benito mussolini established a fascist dictatorship <\s>
<s> his alliance with nazi germany led to italy's defeat in world war ii <\s>
<s> a democratic republic replaced the monarchy in 1946 and economic revival followed <\s>
<s> italy was a charter member of nato and the european economic community eec <\s>
<s> it has been at the forefront of european economic and political unification joining the economic and monetary union in 1999 <\s>
<s> persistent problems include illegal immigration organized crime corruption high unemployment sluggish economic growth and the low incomes and technical standards of southern italy compared with the prosperous north <\s>
<s> jamaica the island discovered by christopher columbus in 1494 was settled by the spanish early in the 16th century <\s>
<s> the native taino indians who had inhabited jamaica for centuries were gradually exterminated and replaced by african slaves <\s>
<s> england seized the island in 1655 and established a plantation economy based on sugar cocoa and coffee <\s>
<s> the abolition of slavery in 1834 freed a quarter million slaves many of whom became small farmers <\s>
<s> jamaica gradually obtained increasing independence from britain <\s>
<s> in 1958 it joined other british caribbean colonies in forming the federation of the west indies <\s>
<s> jamaica gained full independence when it withdrew from the federation in 1962 <\s>
<s> deteriorating economic conditions during the 1970s led to recurrent violence as rival gangs affiliated with the major political parties evolved into powerful organized crime networks involved in international drug smuggling and money laundering <\s>
<s> violent crime drug trafficking and poverty pose significant challenges to the government today <\s>
<s> nonetheless many rural and resort areas remain relatively safe and contribute substantially to the economy <\s>
<s> jan mayen this desolate arctic mountainous island was named after a dutch whaling captain who indisputably discovered it in 1614 earlier claims are inconclusive <\s>
<s> visited only occasionally by seal hunters and trappers over the following centuries the island came under norwegian sovereignty in 1929 <\s>
<s> the long dormant beerenberg volcano resumed activity in 1970 the most recent eruption occurred in 1985 <\s>
<s> it is the northernmost active volcano on earth <\s>

<s> kazakhstan ethnic kazakhs a mix of turkic and mongol nomadic tribes who migrated into the region in the 13th century were rarely united as a single nation <\s>
<s> the area was conquered by russia in the 18th century and kazakhstan became a soviet republic in 1936 <\s>
<s> during the 1950s and 1960s agricultural virgin lands program soviet citizens were encouraged to help cultivate kazakhstan's northern pastures <\s>
<s> this influx of immigrants mostly russians but also some other deported nationalities skewed the ethnic mixture and enabled non-ethnic kazakhs to outnumber natives <\s>
<s> independence in 1991 drove many of these newcomers to emigrate <\s>
<s> kazakhstan's economy is larger than those of all the other central asian states largely due to the country's vast natural resources <\s>
<s> current issues include developing a cohesive national identity expanding the development of the country's vast energy resources and exporting them to world markets diversifying the economy outside the oil gas and mining sectors enhancing kazakhstan's economic competitiveness developing a multiparty parliament and advancing political and social reform and strengthening relations with neighboring states and other foreign powers <\s>
<s> kenya founding president and liberation struggle icon jomo kenyatta led kenya from independence in 1963 until his death in 1978 when president daniel toroitich arap moi took power in a constitutional succession <\s>
<s> the country was a de facto one-party state from 1969 until 1982 when the ruling kenya african national union kanu made itself the sole legal party in kenya <\s>
<s> moi acceded to internal and external pressure for political liberalization in late 1991 <\s>
<s> the ethnically fractured opposition failed to dislodge kanu from power in elections in 1992 and 1997 which were marred by violence and fraud but were viewed as having generally reflected the will of the kenyan people <\s>
<s> president moi stepped down in december 2002 following fair and peaceful elections <\s>
<s> mwai kibaki running as the candidate of the multiethnic united opposition group the national rainbow coalition narc defeated kanu candidate uhuru kenyatta and assumed the presidency following a campaign centered on an anticorruption platform <\s>
<s> kibaki's narc coalition splintered in 2005 over the constitutional review process <\s>
<s> government defectors joined with kanu to form a new opposition coalition the orange democratic movement which defeated the government's draft constitution in a popular referendum in november 2005 <\s>
<s> kibaki's reelection in december 2007 brought charges of vote rigging from odm candidate raila odinga and unleashed two months of violence in which as many as 1,500 people died <\s>
<s> un-sponsored talks in late february produced a powersharing accord bringing odinga into the government in the restored position of prime minister <\s>
<s> kiribati the gilbert islands became a british protectorate in 1892 and a colony in 1915 they were captured by the japanese in the pacific war in 1941 <\s>
<s> the islands of makin and tarawa were the sites of major us amphibious victories over entrenched japanese garrisons in 1943 <\s>
<s> the gilbert islands were granted self-rule by the uk in 1971 and complete independence in 1979 under the new name of kiribati <\s>
<s> the us relinquished all claims to the sparsely inhabited phoenix and line island groups in a 1979 treaty of friendship with kiribati <\s>
<s> korea north an independent kingdom for much of its long history korea was occupied by japan beginning in 1905 following the russo-japanese war <\s>
<s> five years later japan formally annexed the entire peninsula <\s>
<s> following world war ii korea was split with the northern half coming under soviet-sponsored communist control <\s>
<s> after failing in the korean war 1950-53 to conquer the us-backed republic of korea rok in the southern portion by force north korea dprk under its founder president kim il sung adopted a policy of ostensible diplomatic and economic self-reliance as a check against outside influence <\s>
<s> the dprk demonized the us as the ultimate threat to its social system through state-funded propaganda and molded political economic and military policies around the core ideological objective of eventual unification of korea under pyongyang's control <\s>
<s> kim's son the current ruler kim jong il was officially designated as his father's successor in 1980 assuming a growing political and managerial role until the elder kim's death in 1994 <\s>
<s> after decades of economic mismanagement and resource misallocation the dprk since the mid 1990s has relied heavily on international aid to feed its population <\s>
<s> north korea's history of regional military provocations proliferation of military-related items long-range missile development wmd programs including tests of nuclear devices in 2006 and 2009 and massive conventional armed forces are of major concern to the international community <\s>
<s> korea south an independent korean state or collection of states has existed almost continuously for several millennia <\s>
<s> between its initial unification in the 7th century from three predecessor korean states until the 20th century korea existed as a single independent country <\s>
<s> in 1905 following the russo-japanese war korea became a protectorate of imperial japan and in 1910 it was annexed as a colony <\s>
<s> korea regained its independence following japan's surrender to the united states in 1945 <\s>
<s> after world war ii a republic of korea rok was set up in the southern half of the korean peninsula while a communist-style government was installed in the north the dprk <\s>
<s> during the korean war 1950-53 us troops and un forces fought alongside soldiers from the rok to defend south korea from dprk attacks supported by china and the soviet union <\s>
<s> an armistice was signed in 1953 splitting the peninsula along a demilitarized zone at about the 38th parallel <\s>
<s> thereafter south korea achieved rapid economic growth with per capita income rising to roughly 17 times the level of north korea <\s>
<s> in 1993 kim young-sam became south korea's first civilian president following 32 years of military rule <\s>
<s> in keeping with the framework established at the madrid conference in october 1991 bilateral negotiations were conducted between israel and palestinian representatives and syria to achieve a permanent settlement <\s>
<s> israel and palestinian officials signed on 13 september 1993 a declaration of principles also known as the oslo accords guiding an interim period of palestinian self-rule <\s>
<s> outstanding territorial and other disputes with jordan were resolved in the 26 october 1994 israel-jordan treaty of peace <\s>
<s> in addition on 25 may 2000 israel withdrew unilaterally from southern lebanon which it had occupied since 1982 <\s>
<s> in april 2003 us president bush working in conjunction with the eu un and russia the quartet took the lead in laying out a roadmap to a final settlement of the conflict by 2005 based on reciprocal steps by the two parties leading to two states israel and a democratic palestine <\s>
<s> however progress toward a permanent status agreement was undermined by israeli-palestinian violence between september 2003 and february 2005 <\s>
<s> in the summer of 2005 israel unilaterally disengaged from the gaza strip evacuating settlers and its military while retaining control over most points of entry into the gaza strip <\s>
<s> the election of hamas to head the palestinian legislative council froze relations between israel and the palestinian authority pa <\s>
<s> ehud olmert became prime minister in march 2006 and presided over a 34 day conflict with hizballah in lebanon in june-august 2006 and a 23 day conflict with hamas in the gaza strip during december 2008 and january 2009 <\s>
<s> olmert who in june 2007 resumed talks with pa president mahmoud abbas resigned in september 2008 <\s>
<s> prime minister binyamin netanyahu formed a coalition in march 2009 following a february 2009 general election <\s>
<s> direct talks launched in september 2010 collapsed following the expiration of israel's 10 month partial settlement construction moratorium in the west bank <\s>
<s> diplomatic initiatives to revive the negotiations through proximity talks began at the end of 2010 <\s>
<s> italy italy became a nation-state in 1861 when the regional states of the peninsula along with sardinia and sicily were united under king victor emmanuel ii <\s>
<s> an era of parliamentary government came to a close in the early 1920s when benito mussolini established a fascist dictatorship <\s>
<s> his alliance with nazi germany led to italy's defeat in world war ii <\s>
<s> a democratic republic replaced the monarchy in 1946 and economic revival followed <\s>
<s> italy was a charter member of nato and the european economic community eec <\s>
<s> it has been at the forefront of european economic and political unification joining the economic and monetary union in 1999 <\s>
<s> persistent problems include illegal immigration organized crime corruption high unemployment sluggish economic growth and the low incomes and technical standards of southern italy compared with the prosperous north <\s>
<s> jamaica the island discovered by christopher columbus in 1494 was settled by the spanish early in the 16th century <\s>
<s> the native taino indians who had inhabited jamaica for centuries were gradually exterminated and replaced by african slaves <\s>
<s> england seized the island in 1655 and established a plantation economy based on sugar cocoa and coffee <\s>
<s> the abolition of slavery in 1834 freed a quarter million slaves many of whom became small farmers <\s>
<s> jamaica gradually obtained increasing independence from britain <\s>
<s> in 1958 it joined other british caribbean colonies in forming the federation of the west indies <\s>
<s> jamaica gained full independence when it withdrew from the federation in 1962 <\s>
<s> deteriorating economic conditions during the 1970s led to recurrent violence as rival gangs affiliated with the major political parties evolved into powerful organized crime networks involved in international drug smuggling and money laundering <\s>
<s> violent crime drug trafficking and poverty pose significant challenges to the government today <\s>
<s> nonetheless many rural and resort areas remain relatively safe and contribute substantially to the economy <\s>
<s> jan mayen this desolate arctic mountainous island was named after a dutch whaling captain who indisputably discovered it in 1614 earlier claims are inconclusive <\s>
<s> visited only occasionally by seal hunters and trappers over the following centuries the island came under norwegian sovereignty in 1929 <\s>
<s> the long dormant beerenberg volcano resumed activity in 1970 the most recent eruption occurred in 1985 <\s>
<s> it is the northernmost active volcano on earth <\s>
<s> japan in 1603 after decades of civil warfare the tokugawa shogunate a military-led dynastic government ushered in a long period of relative political stability and isolation from foreign influence <\s>
<s> for more than two centuries this policy enabled japan to enjoy a flowering of its indigenous culture <\s>
<s> japan opened its ports after signing the treaty of kanagawa with the us in 1854 and began to intensively modernize and industrialize <\s>
<s> during the late 19th and early 20th centuries japan became a regional power that was able to defeat the forces of both china and russia <\s>
<s> it occupied korea formosa taiwan and southern sakhalin island <\s>
<s> in 1931-32 japan occupied manchuria and in 1937 it launched a full-scale invasion of china <\s>
<s> japan attacked us forces in 1941 triggering america's entry into world war ii and soon occupied much of east and southeast asia <\s>
<s> after its defeat in world war ii japan recovered to become an economic power and an ally of the us <\s>
<s> while the emperor retains his throne as a symbol of national unity elected politicians hold actual decision-making power <\s>
<s> following three decades of unprecedented growth japan's economy experienced a major slowdown starting in the 1990s but the country remains a major economic power <\s>
<s> jersey jersey and the other channel islands represent the last remnants of the medieval dukedom of normandy that held sway in both france and england <\s>
<s> these islands were the only british soil occupied by german troops in world war ii <\s>
<s> jersey is a british crown dependency but is not part of the uk or of the european union <\s>
<s> however the uk government is constitutionally responsible for its defense and international representation <\s>
<s> jordan following world war i and the dissolution of the ottoman empire the uk received a mandate to govern much of the middle east <\s>
<s> britain separated out a semi-autonomous region of transjordan from palestine in the early 1920s and the area gained its independence in 1946 it adopted the name of jordan in 1950 <\s>
<s> the country's long-time ruler was king hussein 1953-99 <\s>
<s> a pragmatic leader he successfully navigated competing pressures from the major powers us ussr and uk various arab states israel and a large internal palestinian population <\s>
<s> jordan lost the west bank to israel in the 1967 war and barely managed to defeat palestinian rebels who attempted to overthrow the monarchy in 1970 <\s>
<s> king hussein in 1988 permanently relinquished jordanian claims to the west bank <\s>
<s> in 1989 he reinstituted parliamentary elections and initiated a gradual political liberalization political parties were legalized in 1992 <\s>
<s> in 1994 he signed a peace treaty with israel <\s>
<s> king abdallah ii the son of king hussein assumed the throne following his father's death in february 1999 <\s>
<s> since then he has consolidated his power and undertaken an aggressive economic reform program <\s>
<s> jordan acceded to the world trade organization in 2000 and began to participate in the european free trade association in 2001 <\s>
<s> in 2003 jordan staunchly supported the coalition ouster of saddam in iraq and following the outbreak of insurgent violence in iraq absorbed thousands of displaced iraqis <\s>

<s> korea north an independent kingdom for much of its long history korea was occupied by japan beginning in 1905 following the russo-japanese war <\s>
<s> five years later japan formally annexed the entire peninsula <\s>
<s> following world war ii korea was split with the northern half coming under soviet-sponsored communist control <\s>
<s> after failing in the korean war 1950-53 to conquer the us-backed republic of korea rok in the southern portion by force north korea dprk under its founder president kim il sung adopted a policy of ostensible diplomatic and economic self-reliance as a check against outside influence <\s>
<s> the dprk demonized the us as the ultimate threat to its social system through state-funded propaganda and molded political economic and military policies around the core ideological objective of eventual unification of korea under pyongyang's control <\s>
<s> kim's son the current ruler kim jong il was officially designated as his father's successor in 1980 assuming a growing political and managerial role until the elder kim's death in 1994 <\s>
<s> after decades of economic mismanagement and resource misallocation the dprk since the mid 1990s has relied heavily on international aid to feed its population <\s>
<s> north korea's history of regional military provocations proliferation of military-related items long-range missile development wmd programs including tests of nuclear devices in 2006 and 2009 and massive conventional armed forces are of major concern to the international community <\s>
<s> korea south an independent korean state or collection of states has existed almost continuously for several millennia <\s>
<s> between its initial unification in the 7th century from three predecessor korean states until the 20th century korea existed as a single independent country <\s>
<s> in 1905 following the russo-japanese war korea became a protectorate of imperial japan and in 1910 it was annexed as a colony <\s>
<s> korea regained its independence following japan's surrender to the united states in 1945 <\s>
<s> after world war ii a republic of korea rok was set up in the southern half of the korean peninsula while a communist-style government was installed in the north the dprk <\s>
<s> during the korean war 1950-53 us troops and un forces fought alongside soldiers from the rok to defend south korea from dprk attacks supported by china and the soviet union <\s>
<s> an armistice was signed in 1953 splitting the peninsula along a demilitarized zone at about the 38th parallel <\s>
<s> thereafter south korea achieved rapid economic growth with per capita income rising to roughly 17 times the level of north korea <\s>
<s> in 1993 kim young-sam became south korea's first civilian president following 32 years of military rule <\s>
<s> in keeping with the framework established at the madrid conference in october 1991 bilateral negotiations were conducted between israel and palestinian representatives and syria to achieve a permanent settlement <\s>
<s> israel and palestinian officials signed on 13 september 1993 a declaration of principles also known as the oslo accords guiding an interim period of palestinian self-rule <\s>
<s> outstanding territorial and other disputes with jordan were resolved in the 26 october 1994 israel-jordan treaty of peace <\s>
<s> in addition on 25 may 2000 israel withdrew unilaterally from southern lebanon which it had occupied since 1982 <\s>
<s> in april 2003 us president bush working in conjunction with the eu un and russia the quartet took the lead in laying out a roadmap to a final settlement of the conflict by 2005 based on reciprocal steps by the two parties leading to two states israel and a democratic palestine <\s>
<s> however progress toward a permanent status agreement was undermined by israeli-palestinian violence between september 2003 and february 2005 <\s>
<s> in the summer of 2005 israel unilaterally disengaged from the gaza strip evacuating settlers and its military while retaining control over most points of entry into the gaza strip <\s>
<s> the election of hamas to head the palestinian legislative council froze relations between israel and the palestinian authority pa <\s>
<s> ehud olmert became prime minister in march 2006 and presided over a 34 day conflict with hizballah in lebanon in june-august 2006 and a 23 day conflict with hamas in the gaza strip during december 2008 and january 2009 <\s>
<s> olmert who in june 2007 resumed talks with pa president mahmoud abbas resigned in september 2008 <\s>
<s> prime minister binyamin netanyahu formed a coalition in march 2009 following a february 2009 general election <\s>
<s> direct talks launched in september 2010 collapsed following the expiration of israel's 10 month partial settlement construction moratorium in the west bank <\s>
<s> diplomatic initiatives to revive the negotiations through proximity talks began at the end of 2010 <\s>
<s> italy italy became a nation-state in 1861 when the regional states of the peninsula along with sardinia and sicily were united under king victor emmanuel ii <\s>
<s> an era of parliamentary government came to a close in the early 1920s when benito mussolini established a fascist dictatorship <\s>
<s> his alliance with nazi germany led to italy's defeat in world war ii <\s>
<s> a democratic republic replaced the monarchy in 1946 and economic revival followed <\s>
<s> italy was a charter member of nato and the european economic community eec <\s>
<s> it has been at the forefront of european economic and political unification joining the economic and monetary union in 1999 <\s>
<s> persistent problems include illegal immigration organized crime corruption high unemployment sluggish economic growth and the low incomes and technical standards of southern italy compared with the prosperous north <\s>
<s> jamaica the island discovered by christopher columbus in 1494 was settled by the spanish early in the 16th century <\s>
<s> the native taino indians who had inhabited jamaica for centuries were gradually exterminated and replaced by african slaves <\s>
<s> england seized the island in 1655 and established a plantation economy based on sugar cocoa and coffee <\s>
<s> the abolition of slavery in 1834 freed a quarter million slaves many of whom became small farmers <\s>
<s> jamaica gradually obtained increasing independence from britain <\s>
<s> in 1958 it joined other british caribbean colonies in forming the federation of the west indies <\s>
<s> jamaica gained full independence when it withdrew from the federation in 1962 <\s>
<s> deteriorating economic conditions during the 1970s led to recurrent violence as rival gangs affiliated with the major political parties evolved into powerful organized crime networks involved in international drug smuggling and money laundering <\s>
<s> violent crime drug trafficking and poverty pose significant challenges to the government today <\s>
<s> nonetheless many rural and resort areas remain relatively safe and contribute substantially to the economy <\s>
<s> jan mayen this desolate arctic mountainous island was named after a dutch whaling captain who indisputably discovered it in 1614 earlier claims are inconclusive <\s>
<s> visited only occasionally by seal hunters and trappers over the following centuries the island came under norwegian sovereignty in 1929 <\s>
<s> the long dormant beerenberg volcano resumed activity in 1970 the most recent eruption occurred in 1985 <\s>
<s> it is the northernmost active volcano on earth <\s>
<s> japan in 1603 after decades of civil warfare the tokugawa shogunate a military-led dynastic government ushered in a long period of relative political stability and isolation from foreign influence <\s>
<s> for more than two centuries this policy enabled japan to enjoy a flowering of its indigenous culture <\s>
<s> japan opened its ports after signing the treaty of kanagawa with the us in 1854 and began to intensively modernize and industrialize <\s>
<s> during the late 19th and early 20th centuries japan became a regional power that was able to defeat the forces of both china and russia <\s>
<s> it occupied korea formosa taiwan and southern sakhalin island <\s>
<s> in 1931-32 japan occupied manchuria and in 1937 it launched a full-scale invasion of china <\s>
<s> japan attacked us forces in 1941 triggering america's entry into world war ii and soon occupied much of east and southeast asia <\s>
<s> after its defeat in world war ii japan recovered to become an economic power and an ally of the us <\s>
<s> while the emperor retains his throne as a symbol of national unity elected politicians hold actual decision-making power <\s>
<s> following three decades of unprecedented growth japan's economy experienced a major slowdown starting in the 1990s but the country remains a major economic power <\s>
<s> jersey jersey and the other channel islands represent the last remnants of the medieval dukedom of normandy that held sway in both france and england <\s>
<s> these islands were the only british soil occupied by german troops in world war ii <\s>
<s> jersey is a british crown dependency but is not part of the uk or of the european union <\s>
<s> however the uk government is constitutionally responsible for its defense and international representation <\s>
<s> jordan following world war i and the dissolution of the ottoman empire the uk received a mandate to govern much of the middle east <\s>
<s> britain separated out a semi-autonomous region of transjordan from palestine in the early 1920s and the area gained its independence in 1946 it adopted the name of jordan in 1950 <\s>
<s> the country's long-time ruler was king hussein 1953-99 <\s>
<s> a pragmatic leader he successfully navigated competing pressures from the major powers us ussr and uk various arab states israel and a large internal palestinian population <\s>
<s> jordan lost the west bank to israel in the 1967 war and barely managed to defeat palestinian rebels who attempted to overthrow the monarchy in 1970 <\s>
<s> king hussein in 1988 permanently relinquished jordanian claims to the west bank <\s>
<s> in 1989 he reinstituted parliamentary elections and initiated a gradual political liberalization political parties were legalized in 1992 <\s>
<s> in 1994 he signed a peace treaty with israel <\s>
<s> king abdallah ii the son of king hussein assumed the throne following his father's death in february 1999 <\s>
<s> since then he has consolidated his power and undertaken an aggressive economic reform program <\s>
<s> jordan acceded to the world trade organization in 2000 and began to participate in the european free trade association in 2001 <\s>
<s> in 2003 jordan staunchly supported the coalition ouster of saddam in iraq and following the outbreak of insurgent violence in iraq absorbed thousands of displaced iraqis <\s>
<s> municipal elections were held in july 2007 under a system in which 20 of seats in all municipal councils were reserved by quota for women <\s>
<s> parliamentary elections were held in november 2010 and saw independent pro-government candidates win the vast majority of seats <\s>
<s> kazakhstan ethnic kazakhs a mix of turkic and mongol nomadic tribes who migrated into the region in the 13th century were rarely united as a single nation <\s>
<s> the area was conquered by russia in the 18th century and kazakhstan became a soviet republic in 1936 <\s>
<s> during the 1950s and 1960s agricultural virgin lands program soviet citizens were encouraged to help cultivate kazakhstan's northern pastures <\s>
<s> this influx of immigrants mostly russians but also some other deported nationalities skewed the ethnic mixture and enabled non-ethnic kazakhs to outnumber natives <\s>
<s> independence in 1991 drove many of these newcomers to emigrate <\s>
<s> kazakhstan's economy is larger than those of all the other central asian states largely due to the country's vast natural resources <\s>
<s> current issues include developing a cohesive national identity expanding the development of the country's vast energy resources and exporting them to world markets diversifying the economy outside the oil gas and mining sectors enhancing kazakhstan's economic competitiveness developing a multiparty parliament and advancing political and social reform and strengthening relations with neighboring states and other foreign powers <\s>
<s> kenya founding president and liberation struggle icon jomo kenyatta led kenya from independence in 1963 until his death in 1978 when president daniel toroitich arap moi took power in a constitutional succession <\s>
<s> the country was a de facto one-party state from 1969 until 1982 when the ruling kenya african national union kanu made itself the sole legal party in kenya <\s>
<s> moi acceded to internal and external pressure for political liberalization in late 1991 <\s>
<s> the ethnically fractured opposition failed to dislodge kanu from power in elections in 1992 and 1997 which were marred by violence and fraud but were viewed as having generally reflected the will of the kenyan people <\s>
<s> president moi stepped down in december 2002 following fair and peaceful elections <\s>
<s> mwai kibaki running as the candidate of the multiethnic united opposition group the national rainbow coalition narc defeated kanu candidate uhuru kenyatta and assumed the presidency following a campaign centered on an anticorruption platform <\s>
<s> kibaki's narc coalition splintered in 2005 over the constitutional review process <\s>
<s> government defectors joined with kanu to form a new opposition coalition the orange democratic movement which defeated the government's draft constitution in a popular referendum in november 2005 <\s>
<s> kibaki's reelection in december 2007 brought charges of vote rigging from odm candidate raila odinga and unleashed two months of violence in which as many as 1,500 people died <\s>
<s> un-sponsored talks in late february produced a powersharing accord bringing odinga into the government in the restored position of prime minister <\s>
<s> kiribati the gilbert islands became a british protectorate in 1892 and a colony in 1915 they were captured by the japanese in the pacific war in 1941 <\s>
<s> the islands of makin and tarawa were the sites of major us amphibious victories over entrenched japanese garrisons in 1943 <\s>
